artificial channel : in artifical channels, owners of lands abutting
them have no natural rights to the use of water or to its flow but
may acquire easements; either as against other persons owning
lands above or below, or as against the maker or owner of the
channel. In the latter case the channel should not be temporary
or precarious but must be of a permanent character so that a
grant of an easement by its maker to persons using it may be
